  559. I was lucky enough to get to try the Gillette Venus Snap with Embrace free (Influenster sent me one complimentary for testing purposes!) It's supposed to be super convenient for shaving on the go, and it does come with a convenient carrying case. I'm always on the go so I loved the idea of this product. I tried it out using just water, since it claims you don't need any shave gel. I wet the razor head really well and wet my leg before shaving, but even though I used water it stung to shave. I ended up with razor burn like crazy because I used it to shave my whole leg. And because it hurt while I was shaving, I couldn't get a very close shave and the hair grew back really quickly -- faster than with other razors. The next time I tried it, I rubbed the blue part of the head on my wet leg before I touched the metal blade to my skin, and that helped a little, but it still wasn't an ideal experience (it still hurt, so I still didn't get a super close shave.) The third time I used the Gillette Venus Snap with Embrace, I used it in my own bathroom and used body wash on my leg to lubricate before shaving. Then I got a painless, super close and smooth shave, and the hair grew back much more slowly! I have used it since without any shave gel JUST for touch-ups, like when I'm on the go and realize I missed a strip of hair. So I wouldn't depend on this to shave your entire leg if you don't plan to use anything to lube them up first. But in a pinch on the go, go for it! (I usually have at least a tube of hand lotion in my purse anyway, so you probably can find something to protect your skin for use on the go. Even handsoap in the public ladies bathroom would do the trick!) I WAS NOT COMPENSATED FOR THIS POST, HOWEVER I DID RECEIVE A SAMPLE FOR MY REVIEW.
